CREATE DATABASE dbVMS
GO

USE dbVMS
GO

CREATE TABLE [Budget] (
  [BudgetId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [MoneyBalance] float,
  [ScoreBalance] int
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Account] (
  [AccountId] nvarchar(255) PRIMARY KEY,
  [WardId] int,
  [GroupId] int,
  [Password] nvarchar(255),
  [Name] nvarchar(255),
  [Gender] bit,
  [BirthDate] datetime,
  [Address] nvarchar(255),
  [Email] nvarchar(255),
  [Phone] nvarchar(255),
  [Avatar] nvarchar(255),
  [Description] nvarchar(255),
  [Reliability] int,
  [MoneyBalance] float,
  [ScoreBalance] int,
  [IsActive] bit,
  [IsDeleted] bit,
  [SearchContent] nvarchar(255),
  [CreatedDate] datetime,
  [UpdatedDate] datetime
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Group] (
  [GroupId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [Name] nvarchar(255),
  [IsDeleted] bit,
  [CreatedDate] datetime,
  [CreatedBy] nvarchar(255),
  [UpdatedDate] datetime,
  [UpdatedBy] nvarchar(255)
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Permission] (
  [GroupId] int,
  [FunctionId] int,
  PRIMARY KEY ([GroupId], [FunctionId])
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Function] (
  [FunctionId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [Code] nvarchar(255),
  [Description] nvarchar(255),
  [IsActive] bit,
  [IsDeleted] bit,
  [CreatedDate] datetime,
  [CreatedBy] nvarchar(255),
  [UpdatedDate] datetime,
  [UpdatedBy] nvarchar(255)
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Post] (
  [PostId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [AccountId] nvarchar(255),
  [Thumbnail] nvarchar(255),
  [Title] nvarchar(255),
  [Author] nvarchar(255),
  [Content] nvarchar(255),
  [Tags] nvarchar(255),
  [Likes] int,
  [Loves] int,
  [Dislikes] int,
  [Status] int,
  [IsDeleted] bit,
  [SearchContent] nvarchar(255),
  [CreatedDate] datetime,
  [UpdatedDate] datetime
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Comment] (
  [CommentId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [AccountId] nvarchar(255),
  [PostId] int,
  [Content] nvarchar(255),
  [BlockReason] nvarchar(255),
  [Likes] int,
  [Loves] int,
  [Dislikes] int,
  [IsDeleted] bit,
  [CreatedDate] datetime,
  [UpdatedDate] datetime
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Campaign] (
  [CampaignId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [AccountId] nvarchar(255),
  [CategoryId] int,
  [WardId] int,
  [Name] nvarchar(255),
  [Image] nvarchar(255),
  [Description] nvarchar(255),
  [Participation] int,
  [Location] nvarchar(255),
  [MoneyBalance] float,
  [ScoreBalance] int,
  [Type] int,
  [Status] int,
  [IsDeleted] bit,
  [SearchContent] nvarchar(255),
  [RegistrationStartDate] datetime,
  [RegistrationEndDate] datetime,
  [ExecutionStartDate] datetime,
  [ExecutionEndDate] datetime,
  [CreatedDate] datetime,
  [UpdatedDate] datetime
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Attendance] (
  [AttendanceId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [AccountId] nvarchar(255),
  [CampaignId] int,
  [Feedback] nvarchar(255)
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Category] (
  [CategoryId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [Name] nvarchar(255),
  [Description] nvarchar(255),
  [IsDeleted] bit,
  [CreatedDate] datetime,
  [CreatedBy] nvarchar(255),
  [UpdatedDate] datetime,
  [UpdatedBy] nvarchar(255)
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [TransactionAC] (
  [TransactionId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [AccountId] nvarchar(255),
  [CampaignId] int,
  [Type] int,
  [MoneyAmount] float,
  [ScoreBalance] int,
  [Content] nvarchar(255),
  [Date] datetime
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [TransactionBA] (
  [TransactionId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [BudgetId] int,
  [AccountId] nvarchar(255),
  [Type] int,
  [MoneyAmount] float,
  [ScoreBalance] int,
  [Content] nvarchar(255),
  [Date] datetime
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [TransactionBC] (
  [TransactionId] int PRIMARY KEY IDENTITY(1, 1),
  [BudgetId] int,
  [CampaignId] int,
  [Type] int,
  [MoneyAmount] float,
  [ScoreBalance] int,
  [Content] nvarchar(255),
  [Date] datetime
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [City] (
  [CityId] int PRIMARY KEY,
  [Code] nvarchar(255),
  [Name] nvarchar(255)
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [District] (
  [DistrictId] int PRIMARY KEY,
  [CityId] int,
  [Code] nvarchar(255),
  [Name] nvarchar(255)
)
GO

CREATE TABLE [Ward] (
  [WardId] int PRIMARY KEY,
  [CityId] int,
  [DistrictId] int,
  [Code] nvarchar(255),
  [Name] nvarchar(255)
)
GO
